	Original rule:

	New rule:
	(-2+i1 >= 0 /\ i6-i4 >= 0 /\ -i5 >= 0 /\ -1-it3+i9 >= 0 /\ i6-i4-i4*(-1+it1386) >= 0 /\ -1-i7+i9 >= 0 /\ 1-i8 >= 0 /\ 2-i1 >= 0 /\ i5 >= 0 /\ -1+it1386 >= 0 /\ -2+i4 >= 0) /\ i1'=i1, i3'=i3+4*it1386, i5'=0, i6'=i6-it1386*i4, i7'=it3, i8'=1

		-2+i1 >= 0 [0]: unchanged
		
		i6-i4 >= 0 [0]: montonic decrease yields (i6-i4 >= 0 /\ i6-i4-i4*(-1+it1386) >= 0), dependencies: -2+i4 >= 0
